<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>SALT LAKE CITY, May 8,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="19" id="led391587F20241261708978150778">2024</a></b> -- Clene Inc. (Nasdaq: CLNN) (along with its subsidiaries, &#8220;Clene&#8221;) and its wholly owned subsidiary Clene Nanomedicine, Inc., a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on revolutionizing the treatment of neurodegenerative diseases, including amyotrophic lateral sclerosis (ALS) and multiple sclerosis (MS), today announced its first quarter 2024 financial results and provided recent operating highlights for the CNM-Au8 clinical program for MS.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&#8220;In the first quarter our team worked diligently to advance our FDA discussions in ALS while continuing to generate more data supporting the neurological benefits and mechanism of action of CNM-Au8,&#8221; said Rob Etherington, President and CEO of Clene. &#8220;We look forward to a productive and collaborative FDA meeting by mid-2024 and laying the groundwork towards filing of a New Drug Application in the second half of the year. Additionally, we are very pleased to see the recent data from our long-term extension of the VISIONARY-MS study. These data represent significant evidence of repair and remyelination across multiple paraclinical endpoints and provide us with greater support for the continued clinical evaluation of CNM-Au8 for this important indication.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b><a data-tblloc="44x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="19" id="led391587F20241261708978169854">First</a> Quarter <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="19" id="led391587F20241261708978158894">2024</a> and Recent Operating Highlights</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><i><b>CNM-Au8 for the treatment of MS</b></i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">In April, the Company announced at the 2024 American Academy of Neurology (AAN) Annual Meeting clinical data demonstrating that long-term CNM-Au8 treatment produced significant evidence of repair and remyelination across multiple paraclinical endpoints. Participants originally randomized to CNM-Au8 treatment experienced continued significant improvement in vision as measured by low contrast letter acuity. More than half of participants improved by 10 or more letters on a low-contrast Sloan eye chart, with increases of up to 38 letters (mixed model repeat measures, or MMRM vs. original baseline, p &lt; 0.001). Study participants treated with CNM-Au8 also experienced up to 29 points of significant improvement (max score =110) in cognition and working memory as measured by the Symbol Digit Modality Test (SDMT) (MMRM vs. original baseline, p &lt; 0.001). Study participants treated with CNM-Au8 also demonstrated functional and structural evidence of repair and remyelination.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">The presentation of Visionary-MS long-term extension results presented at the 2024 AAN Annual Meeting is available <u>here</u>.</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left"><i><b>Corporate Updates</b></i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top;">
			<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: justify; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;">In April, the Company entered into a grant sub-award agreement with Columbia University pursuant to the National Institute of Health (NIH) Grant that includes reimbursement of Company expenses for the NIH Expanded Access Program (EAP) in an amount up to $7.3 million during the period from September 25, 2023&nbsp;to August 31, 2024. In October 2023, the Company announced a four-year, $45.1 million grant from the NIH in collaboration with Columbia University and Synapticure, a neurology specialty health clinic, that is intended to support an EAP for CNM-Au8 treatment of ALS. Disbursement of funds will be paid to Clene based on invoice submissions for reimbursement on a monthly or quarterly basis.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top;">&nbsp;</td>
		</tr>
		<tr>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 27pt; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">&#9679;</td>
			<td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; font-size: 10pt;">In March, Clene announced the publication &#8220;Protein Corona Composition of Gold Nanocatalysts&#8221; in the journal <i>ACS Pharmacology &amp; Translational Science</i>, a journal of the American Chemical Society that publishes innovative and impactful research with translational relevance across a broad spectrum of biological sciences. This corona is an important feature of CNM-Au8&#8217;s neuroprotective mechanism of action and enables the drug&#8217;s longevity in circulation without provoking an inflammatory response.</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; text-align: justify;">The full publication can be accessed here: <u>https://pubs.acs.org/doi/10.1021/acsptsci.4c00028</u></p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left"><b><a data-tblloc="44x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="19" id="led391587F20241261708978169854">First</a> Quarter <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="391587" data-tblv="19" id="led391587F20241261708978158894">2024</a>&nbsp;Financial Results</b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene&#8217;s cash, cash equivalents and marketable securities totaled <a data-tblloc="1x1" data-tblname="394188" data-tblv="19" id="led394188F20234101683735191273" originalfact="$ 27,910,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$27.9 million</a>&nbsp;as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438175058">March 31, 2024</a>, compared to <a data-tblloc="1x2" data-tblname="394188" data-tblv="19" id="led394188F20234101683735196750" originalfact="$ 35,000,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$35.0 million</a>&nbsp;as of <a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438188849">December 31, 2023</a>. Clene expects that its resources as of <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438201114">March 31, 2024</a>, will be sufficient to fund its operations into the fourth quarter of 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Research and development expenses were&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x5" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714502710401" originalfact="$5,869,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$5.9 million</a> for the quarter ended <a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438223925">March 31, 2024</a>, compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x6" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714502723777" originalfact="$7,395,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$7.4 million</a> for the same period in <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438229471">2023</a>.&nbsp;The year-over-year decrease was primarily related to lower expenses related the HEALEY ALS Platform Trial and the RESCUE-ALS, REPAIR-MS, REPAIR-PD, VISIONARY-MS and its long-term extension, and COVID-19 clinical trials, partially offset by an increase in expenses related to the two ongoing EAPs.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">General and administrative expenses were&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x5" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503146359" originalfact="$3,420,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$3.4 million</a> for the quarter ended March 31, 2024, compared to <a data-tblloc="9x6" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503153899" originalfact="$3,439,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$3.4 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in 2023.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">Total other expense was <a data-tblloc="21x5" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503225084" originalfact="$1,848,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$1.8 million</a>&nbsp;for the quarter ended March 31, 2024, compared to total other expense of <a data-tblloc="21x6" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503232646" originalfact="$1,038,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000">$1.0 million</a>&nbsp;for the same period in 2023. The year-over-year increase in expense was primarily attributable to the change in the fair value of our common stock warrant liabilities associated with warrants issued in our financing in June 2023 and warrants issued to Avenue Capital related to our debt facility amendment in June 2023.</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-size: 10pt; text-indent: 0pt; margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; text-align: justify;">Clene reported a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="24x5" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503327603" originalfact="$11,080,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">$11.1 million</a>, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="32x5" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503350298" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">$0.09</a>&nbsp;per share, for the quarter ended&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438223925" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">March 31, 2024</a>, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="24x6" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503334069" originalfact="$11,770,000" scale-include-commas="true" scale-precision="1" scale-round="true" scale-show-unit="true" scale-unit="1000000" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">$11.8 million</a>, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="32x6" data-tblname="391591" data-tblv="19" id="led391591F20243301714503359033" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">$0.15</a>&nbsp;per share, for the same period in&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="391585" data-tblv="19" id="led391585F2023771691438229471" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255); color: rgb(51, 51, 51);">2023</a>.</p>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;"><b>About Clene</b></div>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">Clene Inc., (Nasdaq: CLNN) (along with its subsidiaries, &#8220;Clene&#8221;) and its wholly owned subsidiary Clene Nanomedicine, Inc., is a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on improving mitochondrial health and protecting neuronal function to treat neurodegenerative diseases, including amyotrophic lateral sclerosis, Parkinson&#8217;s disease and multiple sclerosis. CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> is an investigational first-in-class therapy that improves central nervous system cells&#8217; survival and function via a mechanism that targets mitochondrial function and the NAD pathway while reducing oxidative stress. CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> is a federally registered trademark of Clene Nanomedicine, Inc. The company is based in Salt Lake City, Utah, with R&amp;D and manufacturing operations in Maryland. For more information, please visit www.clene.com or follow us on X and LinkedIn.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;"><b>About CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt; text-align: justify;">CNM-Au8 is an oral suspension of gold nanocrystals developed to restore neuronal health and function by increasing energy production and utilization. The catalytically active nanocrystals of CNM-Au8 drive critical cellular energy producing reactions that enable neuroprotection and remyelination by increasing neuronal and glial resilience to disease-relevant stressors. CNM-Au8<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">&#174;</sup> is a federally registered trademark of Clene Nanomedicine, Inc.</p>
